      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses that will occur in the 28th century
       </b>
       . During the period
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2701" title="2701">
        2701
       </a>
       to
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2800" title="2800">
        2800
       </a>
       there will be 242
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Solar_eclipses" title="Solar eclipses">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 84 will be partial, 92 will be annular, 63 will be total, and 3 will be hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year will be five, in 2709 and 2774. One month, May 2785, will have two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div style="clear:both;">
      </div>
